II) come into sight or view
III) be issued or published
IV) seem to be true, probable, or apparent

RESULT: IV) seem to be true, probable, or apparent

IV) hold one's ground; maintain a position; be steadfast or upright
V) put up with something or somebody unpleasant
VI) have or maintain a position or stand on an issue
VII) remain inactive or immobile
VIII) be in effect; be or remain in force
IX) be tall; have a height of; copula
X) put into an upright position
XI) withstand the force of something
XII) be available for stud services

RESULT: I) be standing; be upright
Gold answer is: 3
